23118940_1|23118940|8132|#section_info|0:0|As a starting point we performed a time-course qRT-PCR analysis of the changes in transcript levels of five members of the NF-YA family (NF-YA2, 3, 5, 7, 10), which were up-regulated in our microarray analysis of the Arabidopsis response to low Pi availability [20]. Besides low Pi (5 microM), we also analyzed its response to low N (50 microM), high salinity (100 mM NaCl) and high sucrose (Suc) (9.4%). 23118940_16|23118940|8132|#section_info|0:0|An increase in NF-YA2, NF-YA7 and NF-YA10 transcript levels was detected 4 days after germination (dag) in low P, low N and high Suc treatments, NF-YA5 and NF-YA3 showed a similar response in high Suc but no change in low N and P conditions, respectively (Figure 1). 23118940_20|23118940|8132|#section_info|0:0|An increase in NF-YA2, NF-YA7 and NF-YA10 transcript levels was detected 4 days after germination (dag) in low P, low N and high Suc treatments, NF-YA5 and NF-YA3 showed a similar response in high Suc but no change in low N and P conditions, respectively (Figure 1). Transcript levels were maintained 8 dag and showed a further increase at 14 dag for low P and low N. In high Suc, the level of transcript induction was similar at 8 and 14 dag. This experiment also showed that even though all 5 NF-YAs tested were up-regulated in response to low P, low N and high Suc conditions, the degree of responsiveness of each NF-YA gene to each condition differed, for example, under low N NF-YA3 was the most responsive (19-fold induction at 14dag), whereas NF-YA5 was most responsive in high Suc (43-fold induction at 14dag) and NF-YA10 under low P (51-fold induction at 14 dag).|#main_body|GO:0006995|cellular response to nitrogen starvation|#go_definition|IEP|GOA|NF-YA7(839929)|#gene_synonym

23118940_24|23118940|8132|#section_info|0:0|An increase in NF-YA2, NF-YA7 and NF-YA10 transcript levels was detected 4 days after germination (dag) in low P, low N and high Suc treatments, NF-YA5 and NF-YA3 showed a similar response in high Suc but no change in low N and P conditions, respectively (Figure 1). 23118940_27|23118940|8132|#section_info|0:0|As a starting point we performed a time-course qRT-PCR analysis of the changes in transcript levels of five members of the NF-YA family (NF-YA2, 3, 5, 7, 10), which were up-regulated in our microarray analysis of the Arabidopsis response to low Pi availability [20]. Besides low Pi (5 microM), we also analyzed its response to low N (50 microM), high salinity (100 mM NaCl) and high sucrose (Suc) (9.4%). Transcript levels for these NF-YA family members increased between 5 and 50-fold, under all conditions tested, with the exception of high salinity, where only NF-YA5 and NF-YA3 transcript levels increased by 2-fold at 4 and 14 days of treatment, respectively (Figure 1). |#main_body|GO:0071472|cellular response to salt stress|#go_definition|IEP|GOA|NF-YA3(843614)|#gene_synonym

23118940_29|23118940|8132|#section_info|0:0|An increase in NF-YA2, NF-YA7 and NF-YA10 transcript levels was detected 4 days after germination (dag) in low P, low N and high Suc treatments, NF-YA5 and NF-YA3 showed a similar response in high Suc but no change in low N and P conditions, respectively (Figure 1).
